  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_62dfc390-91ee-4835-9a97-3a9b1b1c8d7f'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText5960214365019203627" style="display:none">A Warrior Of Immortal Powers<br /><br />He was a mighty Scottish warrior who lived in a world bound by ancient laws and timeless magic. But no immortal powers could prepare the laird of Castle Brodie for the lovely accursed lass who stood before him. A terrible trick of fate had sent her 700 years back in time and into his private chamber to tempt him with her beauty—and seduce him with a desire he could never fulfill. For this woman he burned to possess was also<br />the woman he had foresworn to destroy. <br /><br />A Woman Caught In The Mists Of Time<br /><br />When Lisa felt the earth move under her feet, the fiercely independent 21st-century woman never dreamed she was falling...into another century. But the powerful, naked warrior who stood glaring down at her was only too real...and too dangerously arousing. Irresistibly handsome he might be, but Lisa had no intention of remaining in this savage land torn by treachery and war. How could she know that her seductive captor had other plans for her...plans that would save her from a tragic fate? Or that this man who had long ago forsaken love would defy time itself to claim her for his own....</span>

<div id="review_146900930" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/146900930" />
    <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy"><img alt="Kat Kennedy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537750381p2/3270188.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/146900930?book_show_action=true">Feb 08, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kat Kennedy" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy">Kat Kennedy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=romance-romance-romance">romance-romance-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=kat-s-book-reviews">kat-s-book-reviews</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer146900930" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14481791084379825812">In case you're wondering, yes, I am thoroughly ashamed.<br/><br/>How can I possibly give this book more stars than <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2175.Madame_Bovary' title='Madame Bovary by Gustave Flaubert' rel='nofollow noopener'>Madame Bovary</a>? It's disgusting. It's tragic. Worst of all, it doesn't even makes sense. I don't LIKE Historical Romance! <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379758042i/178597.jpg' alt='romance book' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>C'mon, I DARE you to find something dignifying about this.</i><br/><br/>I don't like TIME TRAVEL Historical Romance! I don't like modern woman meets warrior Highlander Hunk. First of all, it's been done - so many times. Never as well as <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10964.Outlander__Outlander___1_' title='Outlander (Outlander, #1) by Diana Gabaldon' rel='nofollow noopener'>Outlander</a>, in my opinion. And I swear, if life imit</span>
  <span id="freeText14481791084379825812" style="display:none">In case you're wondering, yes, I am thoroughly ashamed.<br><br>How can I possibly give this book more stars than <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2175.Madame_Bovary" title="Madame Bovary by Gustave Flaubert" rel="nofollow noopener">Madame Bovary</a>? It's disgusting. It's tragic. Worst of all, it doesn't even makes sense. I don't LIKE Historical Romance! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379758042i/178597.jpg" alt="romance book" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>C'mon, I DARE you to find something dignifying about this.</i><br><br>I don't like TIME TRAVEL Historical Romance! I don't like modern woman meets warrior Highlander Hunk. First of all, it's been done - so many times. Never as well as <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10964.Outlander__Outlander___1_" title="Outlander (Outlander, #1) by Diana Gabaldon" rel="nofollow noopener">Outlander</a>, in my opinion. And I swear, if life imitates fiction then you'd better brush up on your Scottish history because ANY timetravel that is possibly going to occur will not be used to better humanity or learn and introspect about ourselves. No, it's going to be used solely to transport beautiful women back in time to the Highlands to experience a whirlwind romance.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380345404i/700051.jpg" alt="Scotsman" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Get in line, ladies...</i><br><br>And please note to any future Highland authors out there - Kilts were not invented in Scotland until 1725 and specific clan quilts weren't invented until the 19th century. Luckily Moning got one part of this right, in that Circenn wears a plaid, not a kilt (THEY MAY TAKE OUR LAND - BUT THEY'LL NEVER CHAFE... OUR BAAAAAAALLLLLLLLSSSSS!)<br><br>So I was dutifully informed by my harem of adoring lady-lovers that I should skip the first two books and I'm glad I did because I actually really enjoyed this one. Could it, should it and would it ever compare to the indefinable, unsurmountable, incredible Fever series? No, of course not and if you're expecting something quite as awesome then you ARE going to be disappointed. Circenn is no Barrons and whilst Lisa, who starts off making me roll my eyes, is no Mac, she is a reasonable female protagonist.<br><br>What saves this novel is it's interesting conceptualization of the time-honoured Highlander/Timetravel formula, mixed in with a strong, beautiful romance. It was very short of the time-honoured stays of the genre. Lisa doesn't get properly kidnapped ONCE. I know, I know. I was disappointed too. Nor is she ever threatened or almost raped, nor does she actually run away, faint, get lost, lose faith in the male protagonist for some blindingly stupid reason...<br><br>But you know what it's NOT short on?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380345404i/700052.jpg" alt="sex1" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>If you guessed "women playing flaming violins" then you're all out of luck!</i><br><br>That's right. Moning, who I have arbitrarily decided writes brilliant relationship couples, also keeps to her namesake. As in, this book will have you Moning.<br><br>The woman knows how to write sex. It's just all so satisfying!<br><br>And really, if you're reading these kind of books for any other reason, then you really need to re-evaluate your life...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380345404i/700053._SX540_.jpg" alt="violin" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>You may need to discover ANOTHER use for those fingers...</i><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="14481791084379825812" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

           <span class="uitext reviewText">romance lovers</span></div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer26964478" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11792295317345805326">Circenn and Lisa's story - Circenn is a half-human, half-fae man living in the 14th century. He is also immortal thanks to Adam Black slipping the magic Fae liquid that makes humans immortal into his drink when he was in his 30's. Circenn is quite the broody Brud (sorry couldn't resist). He placed a curse on a flask that causes the flask to come back to him. He doesn't realize that his curse will also bring back whoever touches the flask....Enter Lisa, who is working her night time shift in a mu</span>
  <span id="freeText11792295317345805326" style="display:none">Circenn and Lisa's story - Circenn is a half-human, half-fae man living in the 14th century. He is also immortal thanks to Adam Black slipping the magic Fae liquid that makes humans immortal into his drink when he was in his 30's. Circenn is quite the broody Brud (sorry couldn't resist). He placed a curse on a flask that causes the flask to come back to him. He doesn't realize that his curse will also bring back whoever touches the flask....Enter Lisa, who is working her night time shift in a museum as a cleaner. Her curiosity drives her to touch the flask and the next thing she knows she is in a bath with a naked Circenn in the 14th century. Lisa desparately wants to return home to her century because her mother is dying of cancer. Circenn cannot return her because he never learned how to properly use his Fae gifts. Circenn and Lisa fall in love but then Lisa finds out the truth about him ... namely that he is not a simple medieval Brude Scot at all. Great ending to the book, it would be nice to be able to sift around in time and fix things. I loved Circenn as soon as he accepted the magic in his veins.<br /><br /> Circenn wishing good night to Lisa: "Sleep with the angels tonight Lisa. Then come back and sleep with your devil who would burn in hell for one night in your arms." I think that is all that needs to be said about Circenn in that sentence. Bonus to the story: We learn a lot more about Adam Black and get to see him in a more sympathetic light. If you haven't read the Highlander series, I VERY highly recommend you give it a shot. Start with this book, it's great!</span>

<div id="review_45438381" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/45438381" />
    <a title="Dina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1918270-dina"><img alt="Dina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460302951p2/1918270.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/45438381?book_show_action=true">Feb 05, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dina" href="/user/show/1918270-dina">Dina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780440236528" href="/book/show/112753.The_Highlander_s_Touch">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1918270-dina?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1918270-dina?shelf=time-travel">time-travel</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer45438381" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4336333192274235953">Now I understand why "everyone" loves this series! :)<br/><br/>Circenn Brodie is one of the most "delicious" heroes I've ever met. Truly tall, dark & handsome! The scene where Lisa finds him sleeping at her bedroom door had me melting into a puddle of love. It reminded me of a similar scene from Kinley MacGregor's <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/247093.Born_in_Sin__Brotherhood_MacAllister___3_' title='Born in Sin (Brotherhood/MacAllister, #3) by Kinley MacGregor' rel='nofollow noopener'>Born in Sin</a> and, come to think of it, Circenn's nickname was practically identical to MacGregor's hero's name in the same book, but I didn't mind it at all. I'm in love with Circenn and that's a</span>
  <span id="freeText4336333192274235953" style="display:none">Now I understand why "everyone" loves this series! :)<br /><br />Circenn Brodie is one of the most "delicious" heroes I've ever met. Truly tall, dark &amp; handsome! The scene where Lisa finds him sleeping at her bedroom door had me melting into a puddle of love. It reminded me of a similar scene from Kinley MacGregor's <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/247093.Born_in_Sin__Brotherhood_MacAllister___3_" title="Born in Sin (Brotherhood/MacAllister, #3) by Kinley MacGregor" rel="nofollow noopener">Born in Sin</a> and, come to think of it, Circenn's nickname was practically identical to MacGregor's hero's name in the same book, but I didn't mind it at all. I'm in love with Circenn and that's all that matters, LOL.<br /><br />I liked Lisa too, but to a lesser extent - after all, who could top Circenn? :) Lisa was strong and brave, the perfect match for Circenn, and it was easy to relate to her indecision when she had to choose between staying with Circenn or going back to her mother. Seeing that her curiosity was the cause of her time-traveling in the first place, it was funny to see this trait of her pulling her into other "problematic" situations throughout the book.<br /><br />I was never a big fan of time-travel stories, because you can really get "crazy" if you try to analyze all the possibilities behind this concept, but KMM made it work for me. When Circenn "explained" what could and what could not be changed when messing around with time-traveling, I was sold. <i>"If one looks down the timeline, one can discern which things are irrevocable and should not be manipulated, and which things will make little difference."</i> That said, I must admit to being slighlty annoyed with <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Circenn changing five years of Lisa's life in order to make everything - and I mean, <i>everything</i> - right and perfect for her. "Resurrecting" her father was a bit too much, IMHO. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Anyway, if that was to prove how much Circenn loved Lisa, it was fine by me. :)<br /><br />Despite all its "flaws", I <i>loved</i> this book and will definitely read the rest of the series!<br /><br />Random thought: I'm a bit curious about Duncan Douglas, one of the secondary characters. There was a hint of something "good" about to happen to him, but no closure. I wonder if "his" story will be told later in the series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4336333192274235953" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780440236528" href="/book/show/112753.The_Highlander_s_Touch">review of another edition</a>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=reviewed-by-me">reviewed-by-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=author-karen-marie-moning">author-karen-marie-moning</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=series-highlander-moning">series-highlander-moning</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer148879388" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16277364506734810314"><br/><i>The Highlander’s Touch</i> is the third book in Karen Marie Moning’s <i>Highlander</i> series and once again we’re back with a heavy time travel influence. But this time, whether because I’m getting used to it or perhaps it was better written, the time travel didn’t bother me as much as it did in <i>Beyond the Highland Mist</i> and other time travel books I’ve read. I really do hope it’s just me becoming more comfortable with the theme, because it seems I’m missing out on a lot of great Highlander tales.<br/><br/>I thought</span>
  <span id="freeText16277364506734810314" style="display:none"><br /><i>The Highlander’s Touch</i> is the third book in Karen Marie Moning’s <i>Highlander</i> series and once again we’re back with a heavy time travel influence. But this time, whether because I’m getting used to it or perhaps it was better written, the time travel didn’t bother me as much as it did in <i>Beyond the Highland Mist</i> and other time travel books I’ve read. I really do hope it’s just me becoming more comfortable with the theme, because it seems I’m missing out on a lot of great Highlander tales.<br /><br />I thought this story was pretty good, and I found myself laughing out loud a few times. The relationship between our hero and heroine, and for me, one of the high points of the story was seeing <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Adam get a small bit of comeuppance,  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> though long over due and not nearly enough in my oh, so humble opinion.<br /><br />I’m looking forward to continuing this series.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16277364506734810314" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_128861478" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/128861478" />
    <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352609417p2/2489554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/128861478?book_show_action=true">Nov 01, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog) by: </span>
      Angela
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=author-karen-marie-moning">author-karen-marie-moning</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-historical-romance">genre-historical-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=drinks-on-me">drinks-on-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=king-of-the-harem">king-of-the-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=my-hottie-harem">my-hottie-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=the-hymen-club">the-hymen-club</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-go-rabid-over">books-i-go-rabid-over</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer128861478" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12441845401622895286"><b>Posted on<a href='http://underthecoversbookblog.blogspot.com/2012/02/review-highlanders-touch-by-karen-marie.html' rel='nofollow noopener'> Under the Covers</a></b><br/><br/>If a cursed flask holding an immortal elixir is what it takes to travel back in time to find a Highlander hottie like Circenn, then I’m getting my butt on the next train to the museum!<br/><br/>Lisa Stone is twenty-three years old. Her mother, Catherine is sick with cancer and solely relies on her daughter to provide for her in her dying days. Instead of attending college with her friends, Lisa works two jobs, one of which is at a museum. Little does Lisa know that the ancient fl</span>
  <span id="freeText12441845401622895286" style="display:none"><b>Posted on<a href="http://underthecoversbookblog.blogspot.com/2012/02/review-highlanders-touch-by-karen-marie.html" rel="nofollow noopener"> Under the Covers</a></b><br /><br />If a cursed flask holding an immortal elixir is what it takes to travel back in time to find a Highlander hottie like Circenn, then I’m getting my butt on the next train to the museum!<br /><br />Lisa Stone is twenty-three years old. Her mother, Catherine is sick with cancer and solely relies on her daughter to provide for her in her dying days. Instead of attending college with her friends, Lisa works two jobs, one of which is at a museum. Little does Lisa know that the ancient flask before her is cursed to be returned to its owner once it is found. Unfortunately, Circenn didn’t anticipate that the person who touches it will also be transported to him. Back to the 1300’s.<br /><br />Circenn is an honourable man, driven by rules and vows. But when this woman tells him she is from the future, Circenn doesn’t know how to deal with her. He is obligated to kill her by his vow with Adam Black, but when he puts his blade to her throat, his steady hands shakes. <br /><br />It is Lisa’s presence in Circenn’s world that causes him to question himself. I found that I instantly had a connection with Lisa. The life she leaves in the twenty-first century isn’t really hers. Instead, she lives for the benefit of others. Here, in the 1300’s she has a chance to be herself and live the life she had always dreamed of having.<br /><br /><i>“I can’t die now,” she whispered. “I haven’t even lived yet.”</i><br /><br />Moning has a knack for writing witty dialogue. Not only was the bitter back-and-forth banter between Lisa and Circenn amusing, it worked in slowly building up sexual tension that was combustible by the end. I found myself grinning from ear-to-ear while reading this book and laughing out loud at other parts. A book that can evoke any kind of emotion is one that is special.<br /><br /><i>“The gown was too small,” she managed.<br />“I see. And you astutely concluded this would cover more of you?”<br />“I was just about to put my j-jeans back on,” she informed his chest.<br />“I think not.”</i><br /><br />I wondered how Moning would overcome the obstacles she has placed before her heroine. With this time-travel romance, Lisa must choose to either go back to the twenty-first century to care for her mother or remain in medieval Scotland to be with Circenn. The question is, what can’t she live without? Her family or Circenn?<br /><br />Moning drapes a rich background with the historical facts she has incorporated into this story and paired with a hero and heroine that are to die for, I found myself wishing the end never came. <br /><br />Now I <i>really</i> must find a cursed flask!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12441845401622895286" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I'm honestly not sure if would have continued the series had I read the first three books in the series first. Books four, five, and six are my favorite, with book six, The Immortal Highlander, my favorite of the series. You must, however, read books four, five, six, and seven in order. <br/><br/><b>I recommend reading th</b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3305997098631631670">I really enjoyed the conflict and complexity of these characters, Circen is immortal and hates it in a way that makes the costs of immortality feel very real. Adam black, who appeared in earlier books in this series as a one dimensional troublemaker gets significantly more depth here and we discover things about his history. Lisa, the heroine of the story, is grappling with death in her own way, she is plucked from her 21st century life and pulled back in time to meet Circen while trying to supp</span>
  <span id="freeText3305997098631631670" style="display:none">I really enjoyed the conflict and complexity of these characters, Circen is immortal and hates it in a way that makes the costs of immortality feel very real. Adam black, who appeared in earlier books in this series as a one dimensional troublemaker gets significantly more depth here and we discover things about his history. Lisa, the heroine of the story, is grappling with death in her own way, she is plucked from her 21st century life and pulled back in time to meet Circen while trying to support her dying mother after losing her father in a tragic car accident. I loved that this book showed some of the inconveniences of medieval life while also allowing Lisa to display wonder at entering a world she has no context for. And that despite the difficulty of her life in the 21st-century Lisa was neither completely thrilled nor completely relieved to find herself in a new time and place.</span>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText618426857761047265" style="display:none"><b>★Book Basics★</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Genre</i>
</b>: - Historical Paranormal Romance<br /><b>

  <i>Love triangle?</i>
</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>

  <i>Rating </i>
</b>- 3.5 rounded up to 4<br /><br /><br /><b>★Review★</b><br /><br />I enjoyed this one so much more then the first two.<br /><br />Liked both main characters and much preferred the story. <br /><br />The romance felt more real than in the first 2 books, and I much preferred that there were not other suitors, as in book 1 and 2, that the heroine uses to make the hero jealous. <br /><br />The issues that I have though, remains as with book 1 and 2. Sometimes the language used (and not by a character gone back in time) is too modern. Although this one had a more realistic historical feel to it.<br /><br />And again, as with book 1, sometimes things are mentioned that seem like they will have an impact on the story, yet nothing comes of it. For example, mentioning that there is now a warrant out on Lisa in her time, nothing ever happens with that - it is one random scene between Lisa's Mom and her friend, which I can see why that was there, but why make it more complicated mentioning warrants, when it is never going to come to anything. <br /><br />And there was a bit with Circenn's friends Galan and particularly Duncan, when it seemed like they were being set up for a romance to happen in this book, or a future book but having looked, there seems to be nothing for them. So again, a scene with Duncan and and "intriguing" woman, that leads nowhere.<br /><br />But overall, a much more enjoyable story than book 1 and 2, with characters I like much more. And an intriguing look into Adam Black's character and how he is more than he appears to be.</span>

<div id="review_92458305" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/92458305" />

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=zzread-july-2010">zzread-july-2010</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer92458305" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11392421436563653212">While cleaning her boss' office, Lisa comes across an artifact. She touches it and is transported back in time to the 14th century where she meets a very naked Scottish warrior.<br/><br/>Sounds great doesn't it? Well it is yet another fun summer read. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/815150.The_Highlander_s_Touch__Highlander___3_' title='The Highlander's Touch (Highlander, #3) by Karen Marie Moning' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Highlander's Touch</a> is the third book in Karen Marie Moning's Highlander series. Once again, we have the tall, well built, muscular hunk of a man as our hero. We have the requisite virgin. Add in a little fae mischief and we have a great way to spend the </span>
  <span id="freeText11392421436563653212" style="display:none">While cleaning her boss' office, Lisa comes across an artifact. She touches it and is transported back in time to the 14th century where she meets a very naked Scottish warrior.<br /><br />Sounds great doesn't it? Well it is yet another fun summer read. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/815150.The_Highlander_s_Touch__Highlander___3_" title="The Highlander's Touch (Highlander, #3) by Karen Marie Moning" rel="nofollow noopener">The Highlander's Touch</a> is the third book in Karen Marie Moning's Highlander series. Once again, we have the tall, well built, muscular hunk of a man as our hero. We have the requisite virgin. Add in a little fae mischief and we have a great way to spend the time waiting for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7304203.Shadowfever__Fever___5_" title="Shadowfever (Fever, #5) by Karen Marie Moning" rel="nofollow noopener">Shadowfever</a> to be published.<br /><br />All kidding aside, I really did enjoy this novel. It was a beautiful romance with some very hot love scenes. I loved the psychic connection between Lisa and Circenn. There was just the right amount of the fae element. Adam Black appears as himself and as a young boy. The juxtaposition of past and present added some interesting humor, especially when Lisa discovers that Circenn had a room full of modern items. And the ending was beautiful...heavy sigh....<br /><br />A great summer read. Going to read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/112754.Kiss_of_the_Highlander__Highlander___4_" title="Kiss of the Highlander (Highlander, #4) by Karen Marie Moning" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss of the Highlander</a> now. Can't seem to get enough of those Highlanders. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11392421436563653212" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_3027349282" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3027349282" />
    <a title="Ashley Labrecque" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/104623398-ashley-labrecque"><img alt="Ashley Labrecque" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581902474p2/104623398.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3027349282?book_show_action=true">Oct 27, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ashley Labrecque" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ashley Labrecque" href="/user/show/104623398-ashley-labrecque">Ashley Labrecque</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/104623398-ashley-labrecque?shelf=absolute-favourites-reread-worthy">absolute-favourites-reread-worthy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3027349282" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10463779664408870403">6/5 ⭐️ if I could! This is my third time reading this book and it impressed once again. KKM is able to capture the PERFECT balance of history, future, paranormal & Scottish lore. Which I truly believe is difficult for anyone to write, let alone have it flow so beautifully. While this book is apart of the highlander series it does a fantastic job of standing alone with nearly zero references to the other books characters. <br/><br/>Both main characters come with a real world of baggage, much like you would</span>
  <span id="freeText10463779664408870403" style="display:none">6/5 ⭐️ if I could! This is my third time reading this book and it impressed once again. KKM is able to capture the PERFECT balance of history, future, paranormal &amp; Scottish lore. Which I truly believe is difficult for anyone to write, let alone have it flow so beautifully. While this book is apart of the highlander series it does a fantastic job of standing alone with nearly zero references to the other books characters. <br /><br />Both main characters come with a real world of baggage, much like you would expect in any modern day relationship. The book builds on the flaws of baggage &amp; how they can slowly be dismantled when you learn to finally open up to those you trust. <br /><br />The male MC Circen Brodie is a delightful person from the hints on visual appearance to his overall “moral man” personality. If you are looking for a romance novel that has a male interest that embodies good morals &amp; honour this is your book. <br /><br />Lisa our female MC is a women who’s be ravaged by bad luck &amp; the endless grind. This shows in her unwillingness to open up and keep everything bottled. It isn’t until she takes a chance with Circen that both of their worlds &amp; baggage begin to surface. But once the two characters fully appear to one another the result is explosive.<br /><br />KKM also is able to weave in Adam our notorious villain Fae. However, she shows us a lighter side of Adam, arguable his human-side. This changes how the readers navigate Adam both in this books immediate context but also the future books to come. By the end of the book it leaves you with pity &amp; a kinship with his character. </span>
  <a data-text-id="10463779664408870403" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer6043983879484244145">3.5 Stars<br/><br/>I loved the beginning. About 30% in everything slowed down to a crawl. Very little action of any kind. Mostly internal thoughts which became repetitive. <br/>Around 70% things picked up again. <br/>The steam is a very, very <i>Slow Burn</i> and while it was <i>Nice</i>, I was a bit disappointed. I expected more from these two characters with all their passion for things.<br/><br/>The ending was a mixed bag. There is a reveal that I sort of expected, but was interesting. It explained a lot about Circen and Adam. <br/><br/>But then</span>
  <span id="freeText6043983879484244145" style="display:none">3.5 Stars<br /><br />I loved the beginning. About 30% in everything slowed down to a crawl. Very little action of any kind. Mostly internal thoughts which became repetitive. <br />Around 70% things picked up again. <br />The steam is a very, very <i>Slow Burn</i> and while it was <i>Nice</i>, I was a bit disappointed. I expected more from these two characters with all their passion for things.<br /><br />The ending was a mixed bag. There is a reveal that I sort of expected, but was interesting. It explained a lot about Circen and Adam. <br /><br />But then things got a bit too jejune for me. I suddenly felt like I was reading a YA story! It became to Disney World. Make a wish, click your heels and POOF, ALL your wishes come true. <br /><br />I liked this one a lot more than the last in the series. <br /><br />Anyway, I will read book #4 next month. But, if it isn't better written than the first 3, I will stop them. Even though I like the characters, there is just to much repetitive thoughts to hold my interest.</span>

<div id="review_16387426" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/16387426" />
    <a title="Eastofoz" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/939365-eastofoz"><img alt="Eastofoz" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1203907098p2/939365.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/16387426?book_show_action=true">Feb 25, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eastofoz" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eastofoz" href="/user/show/939365-eastofoz">Eastofoz</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780440236528" href="/book/show/112753.The_Highlander_s_Touch">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/939365-eastofoz?shelf=highlander">highlander</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/939365-eastofoz?shelf=time-travel">time-travel</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer16387426&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer16387426" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16935535613849349664">Book 3 in Moning's Highlander series is better than 1 and 2 but still lacks some oomph. There's too much narration and not enough dialog at times. Circenn Brodie (great name!) is one sexy Highlander! Think of the most beautiful marble sculpture you've ever seen and that's Circenn--pure eye candy! The one off thing about him that he's 6'7! That's gigantic even if he is an immortal!<br/><br/>Lisa, the heroine, is a bit drab and some of the things she says or does reminded me a toddler stamping their feet in</span>
  <span id="freeText16935535613849349664" style="display:none">Book 3 in Moning's Highlander series is better than 1 and 2 but still lacks some oomph. There's too much narration and not enough dialog at times. Circenn Brodie (great name!) is one sexy Highlander! Think of the most beautiful marble sculpture you've ever seen and that's Circenn--pure eye candy! The one off thing about him that he's 6'7! That's gigantic even if he is an immortal!<br /><br />Lisa, the heroine, is a bit drab and some of the things she says or does reminded me a toddler stamping their feet in frustration. It seemed strange that she could go back to 14 century Scotland and suddenly start speaking in an older formal English when she's from the 20th century--it's like she didn't miss a step after the initial "shock" wore off. A bit too quick I thought. Circenn is what keeps this book afloat. <br /><br />The steamy-scenes missed the mark each time--almost there but just out of reach of being really good. Even the first time they were "together" wasn't particularly satisfying and seeing as she was a virgin I thought a little more could have been said about her first time. It's almost as if Moning is embarrassed to go into more detail during the love scenes so she side-steps around it. The emotional connection they had was interesting and helped avoid "the big misunderstanding" that plagues too many romance novels.<br /><br />Duncan is a great secondary character--plays the randy male very well! Even Adam comes out looking good when in Book 1 he was such a horrible mean fairy. <br /><br />The ending is what really saves the whole book. A bit of a twist on the time travel romance. Leaves you feeling happy with a smile on your face :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="16935535613849349664" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer547751196" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16969766429401845640"><br/>So, this was the first book in the series that <i>actually</i> had an immortal dude in it. I know, right? A Highlander series where so far only one guy is immortal.<br/>I'll admit it wasn't bad in the beginning, but close to the end is where it took a turn for the, not worse, but totally and completely <b>ridiculous</b>.<br/><br/>I tell you, I practically saw it coming and had to speed read because I couldn't believe she actually tied it up in such a way. <br/><br/>And like the last two books, the heroines always - I repeat, always -</span>
  <span id="freeText16969766429401845640" style="display:none"><br />So, this was the first book in the series that <i>actually</i> had an immortal dude in it. I know, right? A Highlander series where so far only one guy is immortal.<br />I'll admit it wasn't bad in the beginning, but close to the end is where it took a turn for the, not worse, but totally and completely <b>ridiculous</b>.<br /><br />I tell you, I practically saw it coming and had to speed read because I couldn't believe she actually tied it up in such a way. <br /><br />And like the last two books, the heroines always - I repeat, always - end up pregnant. <br />It's like that is the formula for a happily ever after and without it you may as well end the world now.<br /><br />But while Karen Marie Moning can write the romance aspect very well, her stories have plot holes so big I'm surprised I didn't fall into one. I kid you not.<br /><br />In the end, the writing style wasn't horrible and the romance between the H/h wasn't too disgusting so I gave it a 2. Also, due to dialogue and all the "doonas" I was rather enjoying that aspect of it. I like the whole accent thing. Hah.<br /><br />I'll keep reading these books until I get to the very damn last one, I tell ya. I really want to use "doona" in a sentence but I can't think of what to say. Darn it.<br /><br /> <br /><br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_479279977" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/479279977" />
    <a title="Jamie *Gypsy Smut-a-teer*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer"><img alt="Jamie *Gypsy Smut-a-teer*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363047769p2/10459827.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/479279977?book_show_action=true">Dec 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jamie *Gypsy Smut-a-teer*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jamie *Gypsy Smut-a-teer*" href="/user/show/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer">Jamie *Gypsy Smut-a-teer*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer?shelf=love-a-man-in-a-kilt">love-a-man-in-a-kilt</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer?shelf=hea">hea</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer?shelf=other-paranormal">other-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer?shelf=not-so-bad-boy">not-so-bad-boy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer479279977" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7495015065065014708">I'm really really liking this series. I fall in love over again with each character.<br/><br/>Lisa and Circenn meet on less than normal cirumstances. She is a girl from the present with a lot of responsibilty on her shoulders. He is a fierce warrior who is immortal from the fourteenth century. The saying Curiousity kills the Cat is basically right on point in this story. She touches a historical flask of her bosses where she wasn't even supposed to be. The Flask had been cursed sending her straight back t</span>
  <span id="freeText7495015065065014708" style="display:none">I'm really really liking this series. I fall in love over again with each character.<br /><br />Lisa and Circenn meet on less than normal cirumstances. She is a girl from the present with a lot of responsibilty on her shoulders. He is a fierce warrior who is immortal from the fourteenth century. The saying Curiousity kills the Cat is basically right on point in this story. She touches a historical flask of her bosses where she wasn't even supposed to be. The Flask had been cursed sending her straight back through the past into Circenn's chambers where she finds him shocked and naked. With the curse he has made one of many oaths to kill whoever brought it back the second they showed. But Circenn had also made an oath to his mom not to hurt women and another oath that said he wouldn't spill innocent blood. So, what a fix he has found himself in. <br /><br />All Lisa wants is to be sent back home, all Circenn wants is to make sure she is actually innocent and find a way to spare her life. But after an accidental marriage annoucment between the two he sees there will be no way he will be able to stand by his oath. Over time they both start having feelings for one another. Circenn makes his known but Lisa is still torn between being with someone she thinks she is falling for or feeling bad about her mom and trying to find a way home. <br /><br />Circenn was such a Scotish gentleman. He makes his feelings clear but steps back and lets her work through her own. He continues to be a rock for her but also gives her space when he feels its needed. I loved the bond these two ended up having. I thought it was super cool for them to be able to feel what the other is feeling. <br /><br />I must say, I was a little disappointed in the ending. I mean it was perfect. But after reading everything he did for her, I mean he worked some miracles for her I felt the end was lacking. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I wanted to read a little, maybe in the Epilogue, about them sharing there feelings while she was pregnant, or while she was having the baby. I would actually, maybe this is horrible of me, but I really wanted to read about how he felt about the amount of pain she was in while having their baby. It would be the first time in history a man acutally felt what women felt. I wanted to see how he reacted. I also thought after loosing her dad she would have wanted to see him alive. SO, a glimpse into their wedding would have been nice. Or a glimpse into how her parents reacted to going back into the past. There was so much opportunity here and the other two books have given us a glimpse into the future with the happy couple but this one didn't. I was hugely disappointed by this.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Overall, I really liked this book, besides the disappointing ending. I've been told the next three books are the best in the series so I'm excited to start them. I have never been into historical romance AT ALL, but I feel like these are close to it and surprisingly I really like them. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7495015065065014708" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer13441995493590574920">There were a lot of things to like about this book.<br/>Circenn and his insistence on following a few basic rules - until he meets Lisa and starts breaking his own rules one by one. Circenn and his love for his family and his people. Circenn and his old-fashioned morals and gentleness. Circenn and his desire to make Lisa happy.   <span id="freeText13441995493590574920" style="display:none">There were a lot of things to like about this book.<br />Circenn and his insistence on following a few basic rules - until he meets Lisa and starts breaking his own rules one by one. Circenn and his love for his family and his people. Circenn and his old-fashioned morals and gentleness. Circenn and his desire to make Lisa happy. Circenn and...<br /><br />I found it very easy to empathize with Lisa and her problems in the present time, and to respect her because she put aside her dreams to work menial jobs and care for her mother. I liked that Lisa had knowledge of the 14th century &amp; enjoyed 'losing herself' in the medieval wing of the museum - it made it more plausible that she could adapt to medieval life. What I couldn't understand was why she waited so long to explain why she wanted/needed to go back to her own time.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14140755636700008800">3.5/5; 4 stars; B+<br/><br/>I really enjoyed this audiobook. A few years ago I had picked up a different book in this series and didn't care for it so wasn't really expecting too much here. It was a nice surprise to find an intelligent and gutsy heroine and a tough but kindhearted hero. Many parts of this story made me laugh out loud.   <span id="freeText14140755636700008800" style="display:none">3.5/5; 4 stars; B+<br /><br />I really enjoyed this audiobook. A few years ago I had picked up a different book in this series and didn't care for it so wasn't really expecting too much here. It was a nice surprise to find an intelligent and gutsy heroine and a tough but kindhearted hero. Many parts of this story made me laugh out loud. One thing that I enjoyed was coming to understand the character of Adam Black a bit better. He is not the main character in this book but his shenanigans are behind a lot of the events of the story. <br />Phil Gigante narrated this story and did a great job, especially with the accents. </span>

<div id="review_31641718" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/31641718" />
    <a title="Mojca" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1359426-mojca"><img alt="Mojca" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1379576265p2/1359426.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/31641718?book_show_action=true">Aug 31, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mojca" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mojca" href="/user/show/1359426-mojca">Mojca</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1359426-mojca?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1359426-mojca?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1359426-mojca?shelf=paranormal-romance-fantasy">paranormal-romance-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1359426-mojca?shelf=scottish-irish-celtic-hh-setting">scottish-irish-celtic-hh-setting</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1359426-mojca?shelf=karen-marie-moning">karen-marie-moning</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1359426-mojca?shelf=medieval">medieval</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1359426-mojca?shelf=time-travel">time-travel</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer31641718" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2403147836589582959">In 1308 Circenn Brodie, the immortal laird of Brodie, swears an oath to kill whomever comes along with a hallowed Fae flask that's been recently stolen and put a binging spell on.<br/><br/>In present day Cincinnati, Lisa Stone is working two jobs to pay the medical bills for her deathly ill mother. One of those jobs include night cleaning at the museum...Then one morning, curiosity makes her touch a shimmering flask in a recently unearthed chest brought to the US from the Scottish Highlands...and she find</span>
  <span id="freeText2403147836589582959" style="display:none">In 1308 Circenn Brodie, the immortal laird of Brodie, swears an oath to kill whomever comes along with a hallowed Fae flask that's been recently stolen and put a binging spell on.<br /><br />In present day Cincinnati, Lisa Stone is working two jobs to pay the medical bills for her deathly ill mother. One of those jobs include night cleaning at the museum...Then one morning, curiosity makes her touch a shimmering flask in a recently unearthed chest brought to the US from the Scottish Highlands...and she finds herself flung 700 years back, to 1314 and castle Dunnottar, smack in the middle of Circenn Brodie's chambers.<br /><br />Yet the man who swore the oath to kill her, the man who lived his life with honor, cannot bring himself to do what he'd sworn to do. And the woman who, in the past five years, had seldom experienced tenderness, care and comfort finds herself falling for the towering warrior.<br /><br />But there are obligations waiting for her back in the future, and even though Circenn claims he cannot return her, Lisa is adamant in finding a way out of her predicament and back to her mother's side...Even if it means breaking two hearts in the process.<br /><br /><br />This was the first <a href="https://thebookgourmet.blogspot.com/search/label/Karen%20Marie%20Moning" rel="nofollow noopener">Karen Marie Moning</a> book I ever bought, it introduced me to the author and to this <a href="https://thebookgourmet.blogspot.com/p/seriously-serial.html#Highlander" rel="nofollow noopener">series</a>. And yes, it's probably my favorite of them all. You know, you never forget your first one.<br /><br />But what's not to like about this story, really?<br />It's set in Scottish Highlands (my favorite setting of them all; I've actually visited both castles mentioned in this story—Dunnottar and Brodie!), it features, albeit briefly, the battle at Bannock Burn (providing one of the best quotes in this book*), it's filled with wonderful supporting cast (the Douglas Brothers, the surprise appearance of Robert the Bruce in all his matchmaking glory...), and has one hell of a leading man.<br /><br />Circenn Brodie, the ninth-century warrior living in the fourteenth-century war-torn Scotland, falling in love with a twenty-first century woman. And the man was barely ruffled, except when it came to the woman, of course, as it should be.<br />Granted, I'm not really sure why he fell in love with her, she (at least not that I could see) had any special characteristics, except for being "alien" and having a mind of her own. Yes, she's suffered, she had issues, but that was pretty much it. Not much was spent on her character at least not in the way for Circenn to fall for her the way he did.<br />While many pages were spent on Circenn and all his good qualities (did he even have any bad ones), making him known to the reader so that she/he would understand, empathize and sympathize with Lisa's plight as she stumbled over the proverbial cliff.<br /><br />And then there was Adam Black whose real identity, as it was revealed, comes as a huge surprise for those who read this book for the first time. I'm glad he's starting to redeem himself after the "mischief" he concocted in the <a href="https://thebookgourmet.blogspot.com/2018/03/review-beyond-the-highland-mist.html" rel="nofollow noopener">first book</a> (where he was quite a villain) and we're slowly working toward his own story.<br /><br />This book was a fast-paced, intriguing mix of historical romance and time-travel with a gripping, yet minor, suspense and treason sub-plot, the romance was lovely and heartfelt, the narration was wonderfully evocative, painting vivid pictures of the characters and their surroundings...All nicely intertwined with magical elements and the beauty of Scotland.<br /><br /><br />*<blockquote>
  <i>Along the Bannock Burn, Circenn Brodie was an animal, merciless and swift. Later the men would claim he vied with the Berserkers in his deadly rage, and epics would be composed in his honor. He was cold and sharp and hard, and good for nothing but slaughter. He lost himself in a blackness so complete that he cared naught if he slew legions, he simply raged, hoping to exhaust himself and gain the respite of unconsciousness, a temporary kind of death.</i>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="2403147836589582959" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3709091-lover-of-romance?shelf=scottish-highlands">scottish-highlands</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3709091-lover-of-romance?shelf=time-travel">time-travel</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer105346284" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6384434842897165958">Lisa is shocked when, at one of her two jobs, she ends up through her curse of curiosity persay, she ends up being taken back through time, 700 years in Medieval Scotland, with a sword being pointed at her throat. Definitely not what she imagined her day turning out. Circern, when seeing a woman appear before him holding the "flask" he knows he has to remember his vow, and destroy her, but he hesitates thinking that she could be a innocent.Lisa is determined to find a way back to her own time, b</span>
  <span id="freeText6384434842897165958" style="display:none">Lisa is shocked when, at one of her two jobs, she ends up through her curse of curiosity persay, she ends up being taken back through time, 700 years in Medieval Scotland, with a sword being pointed at her throat. Definitely not what she imagined her day turning out. Circern, when seeing a woman appear before him holding the "flask" he knows he has to remember his vow, and destroy her, but he hesitates thinking that she could be a innocent.Lisa is determined to find a way back to her own time, because she has a mother that needs her more now than ever, and she has been taken away from that life and into a different one in the fourteenth century, yet feels a connection to to Circern. So through a series of events, Circern and Lisa end up being handfasted and a passion is awakened unlike anything either one of them has ever experienced before. Yet will they be able to find a way to have.....Forever? <br />The Highlanders Touch is the third installment in the Highland series by Karen Marie Moning. I haven't read the fever series yet, but her highland series I have just fallen for completely. I have enjoyed each of her books in the series so far, especially since I love anything romances to do with the Scottish Highlands. One of the things I didn't expect when I first started reading this one, was how emotional this book would become for the reader, from beginning to end the plot was filled with excitement, adventure and lots of romance. The relationship between the two especially at first is a bit rocky, but there is a connection between the two and we see the first seeds of their love for each other. I loved both of these characters, they were full of depth and likeable. There was also a level of emotion that is portrayed throughout the book, that will touch any reader deeply. I absolutely adored reading this, and was such a magical read!!!<br /><br />My Favorite Quote <br /> Live with me forever. Cease my endless solitude. I will cherish you. I will show you world you only dreamed of. I will walk beside you, hand in hand, until the end of days. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6384434842897165958" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('o8XgUPRpfkaCEzkIoSfLhuQWKqc9Ilx2wKp62NdEwYOQknfl5tJ7Xa5VcU8pk37xwB3zACkxpTOAQxCoNboPtg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer2041643842841245964">“The only other calling I ever felt was an irrepressible desire to be Captain of my own Starship. I was born in the wrong century and it wasn’t possible, so I chose to explore the universe by writing fiction instead. Books are doors to endless adventure.” -KMM<br/><br/>Karen Marie Moning is the #1 NYT bestselling author of the Fever Series and Highlander novels.<br/><br/>An alum of the Immaculate Conception Academy, </span>
  <span id="freeText2041643842841245964" style="display:none">“The only other calling I ever felt was an irrepressible desire to be Captain of my own Starship. I was born in the wrong century and it wasn’t possible, so I chose to explore the universe by writing fiction instead. Books are doors to endless adventure.” -KMM<br /><br />Karen Marie Moning is the #1 NYT bestselling author of the Fever Series and Highlander novels.<br /><br />An alum of the Immaculate Conception Academy, at seventeen she attended Purdue University where she completed a BA in Society &amp; Law, with minors in Philosophy, Creative Writing and Theatre, while working full time as a bartender and computer consultant. She intended to go to law school but after an internship with a firm of Criminal Attorneys, decided against it. For the next decade, she worked in insurance, where she wrote intercompany arbitrations and directed commercial litigation. At the age of thirty, she decided it was time to get serious and do what she’d always wanted to do: write fiction novels.<br /><br />Beyond the Highland Mist was published in 1999 and nominated for two RITA awards. She then published six more novels in her award-winning HIGHLANDER series, and received the RITA Award in 2001 for The Highlander’s Touch.<br /><br />In 2004, she began writing the #1 New York Times bestselling FEVER series. The books have been optioned twice for potential franchise development by Twentieth Century Fox and DreamWorks Studios, but the rights are currently held by Moning who has expressed a desire to one day see it as a television series. Her novels have been published in over thirty countries. She divides her time between Ohio and Florida and is working on two future projects for Random House Publishing.<br /><br />“I have always imagined that Paradise will be a kind of library.” – Jorge Luis Borges</span>

            <span class="readable">&ldquo;He ran a hand over his face and shook his head. "Lass, I have never lied to you. I adore you and there have never been any other women from the future here. And these"- he flung a tampon in the air- "cleaning swabs, I cannot fathom why they upset you so greatly, but I assure you I have never let the maids use them."<br /><br />Lisa's brow furrowed. No man could be so stupid. "Cleaning Swabs?"<br /><br />He snatched up a gun and jerked the barrel in her direction, and an unwrapped tampon shot out. It was coated with black from the slow corrosion of the steel. She eyed it for a moment, bent, and plucked it from the floor. "You clean your guns with these?"<br /><br />He lowered the gun. "Is that not the purpose for which they were designed? I vow I could not conceive of another."<br /><br />Didn't you read the box?"<br /><br />There were too many words I didn't understand!&rdquo;</span>

    n = load.length,

        script.src = load[i];
        first.parentNode.insertBefore(script, first);

    w.attachEvent('onload', go);
  } else {
    w.addEventListener('load', go, false);
